Compliance Reminder: Medical Data Handling Under GDPR/CCPA As part of your duty to protect employee health data, please ensure all communications regarding medical conditions, treatment plans, or medication use are stored in secure, access-restricted folders — never in shared drives or personal email accounts. Even seemingly innocuous messages about therapy schedules or dosage changes qualify as sensitive personal information under data protection laws. Failure to comply may expose the organisation to regulatory penalties. We recommend a short training module for all HR staff this week.

Service Notice: Secure Transfer of Employee Medical Data Our platform now enforces end-to-end encryption for all transmissions involving employee medical information. Adjusting leave policy for international teams – cultural considerations As we expand our operations into regions where kinship care and non-biological adoption are culturally common, our current leave policy risks excluding employees who are legally finalizing family units without a formal adoption decree. In countries like Kenya and the Philippines, raising a relative’s child under customary law is widespread, yet our system doesn’t recognize it. I recommend broadening our definition of qualifying leave to include “permanent familial caregiving arrangements” regardless of legal terminology. This would improve inclusion and reduce attrition among global teams who feel their family structures are invalidated. Let’s discuss how to update the handbook.
